| Package | Version | Deprecation Text |
| ------- | ------- | ---------------- |
| [4-color](https://github.com/zhanzhenzhen/atom-4-color) | 0.2.9 | Store package style sheets in the `styles/` directory instead of `stylesheets/` in the `4-color` package |
| [4-color-dark](https://github.com/zhanzhenzhen/atom-4-color-dark) | 0.1.1 | Store package style sheets in the `styles/` directory instead of `stylesheets/` in the `4-color-dark` package |
| [academic](https://github.com/NickRSearcy/academic) | 0.34.1 | Store package settings files in the `settings/` directory instead of `scoped-properties/` |
| [accents-ui](https://github.com/kieranju/accents-ui) | 0.2.0 | Requiring `$` from `atom` is no longer supported. If you are using `space-pen`, please require `$` from `atom-space-pen-views`. Otherwise require `jquery` instead: `{$} = require 'atom-space-pen-views'` or `$ = require 'jquery'` Add `"atom-space-pen-views": "^2.0.3"` to your package dependencies. Or add `"jquery": "^2"` to your package dependencies. |
| [accents-ui](https://github.com/kieranju/accents-ui) | 0.2.0 | Requiring `View` from `atom` is no longer supported. Please require `atom-space-pen-views` instead: `{View} = require 'atom-space-pen-views'` Add `"atom-space-pen-views": "^2.0.3"` to your package dependencies. |
| [accents-ui](https://github.com/kieranju/accents-ui) | 0.2.0 | Requiring `EditorView` from `atom` is no longer supported. Please require `TextEditorView` from `atom-space-pen-view` instead: `{TextEditorView} = require 'atom-space-pen-views'` Add `"atom-space-pen-views": "^2.0.3"` to your package dependencies. |
| [acf-snippets](https://github.com/emaildano/acf-snippets) | 0.6.0 | Store package style sheets in the `styles/` directory instead of `stylesheets/` in the `acf-snippets` package |
| [acf-snippets](https://github.com/emaildano/acf-snippets) | 0.6.0 | Use `activationCommands` instead of `activationEvents` in your package.json Commands should be grouped by selector as follows: ```json "activationCommands": { "atom-workspace": ["foo:bar", "foo:baz"], "atom-text-editor": ["foo:quux"] } ``` |
| [advanced-new-file](https://github.com/Trudko/advanced-new-file) | 0.4.3 | Use TextEditor::getLastSelection() instead |
| [advanced-open-file](https://github.com/Osmose/advanced-open-file) | 0.6.0 | Store package style sheets in the `styles/` directory instead of `stylesheets/` in the `advanced-open-file` package |

The global was previously being assigned by the status-bar package, but Atom packages should never assign globals. In the future, this problem will be solved by an inter-package communication API available on `atom.services`. For now, you can get a reference to the `status-bar` element via `document.querySelector('status-bar')`. |
